CREATE TABLE Member(
memberId 	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
memberName 		varchar(30) NOT NULL,
email 		varchar(30) NOT NULL,
memberPhoneNo 	varchar(11) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (memberId)
);

CREATE TABLE Item(
itemId  	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
itemName 	varchar(30) NOT NULL,
category 	varchar(20) NOT NULL,
itemPrice number(7,2) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (itemId)
);

CREATE TABLE Staff(
staffId 	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
staffName  	varchar(30) NOT NULL,
role  		varchar(20) NOT NULL,
staffPhoneNo 	varchar(11) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (staffId)
);

CREATE TABLE Part(
partId  	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
partName 	varchar(20) NOT NULL,
partCost  	number(7,2) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (partId)
);

CREATE TABLE Insurance(
insuranceId 	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
insuranceDescription 	varchar(50) NOT NULL,
insuranceType	 varchar(30) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (insuranceId)
);

CREATE TABLE Airplane(
airplaneId  	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
model  		varchar(15) NOT NULL,
capacity  	number 	NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (airplaneId)
);

CREATE TABLE Passenger(
passengerIC  	varchar(14) NOT NULL,
passengerName 	varchar(30) NOT NULL,
email 		varchar(30) NOT NULL,
passengerPhoneNo varchar(11) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (passengerIC)
);

CREATE TABLE Maintenance(
maintainDate  	date NOT NULL,
partId  	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
airplaneId  	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
description varchar(30) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (maintainDate, partId, airplaneId),
FOREIGN KEY (partId) REFERENCES Part(partId),
FOREIGN KEY (airplaneId) REFERENCES Airplane(airplaneId)
);

CREATE TABLE Flight(
flightId  varchar(4) NOT NULL,
airplaneId  	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
origin  	varchar(20) NOT NULL,
destination 	varchar(20) NOT NULL,
departureTime  	varchar(10) NOT NULL,
arrivalTime  	varchar(10) NOT NULL,
flightDate 	date NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (flightId),
FOREIGN KEY (airplaneId) REFERENCES Airplane(airplaneId)
);

CREATE TABLE Seat(
seatId 		varchar(8) NOT NULL,
flightId 	varchar(4) NOT NULL,
seatType 	varchar(15) NOT NULL,
season   varchar(20) NOT NULL,
price number(7,2) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (seatId),
FOREIGN KEY (flightId) REFERENCES Flight(flightId)
);

CREATE TABLE InsurancePolicy(
policyId 	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
insuranceId  	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
expiredDate  	date NOT NULL,
coverageAmount 	number(7,2) NOT NULL,
details 	varchar(50) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (policyId),
FOREIGN KEY (insuranceId) REFERENCES Insurance(insuranceId)
);

CREATE TABLE InsuranceClaim(
claimId  	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
policyId  	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
claimDate 	date NOT NULL,
claimAmount 	number(7,2) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (claimId),
FOREIGN KEY (policyId) REFERENCES InsurancePolicy(policyId)
);

CREATE TABLE FlightDelay(
delayId 	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
flightId  	varchar(4) NOT NULL,
reason  	varchar(30),
delayDuration   varchar(10) NOT NULL,
newDepartureTime  	varchar(10) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (delayId),
FOREIGN KEY (flightId) REFERENCES Flight(flightId)
);

CREATE TABLE Workload(
flightId		varchar(4)  NOT NULL,
staffId     		varchar(5) NOT NULL,
taskDescription  	varchar(30) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (flightId, staffId),
FOREIGN KEY (flightId) REFERENCES Flight(flightId),
FOREIGN KEY (staffId) REFERENCES Staff(staffId)
);

CREATE TABLE Booking(
bookingId 	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
memberId 	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
status 		varchar(10) NOT NULL,
bookingDate 	date NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (bookingId),
FOREIGN KEY (memberId) REFERENCES Member(memberId)
);

CREATE TABLE Payment(
paymentId 	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
bookingId 	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
paymentDate 	date 	NOT NULL,
paymentAmount 		number(7,2) NOT NULL,
paymentMethod 	varchar(20) NOT NULL,
paymentStatus 	varchar(20) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (paymentId),
FOREIGN KEY (bookingId) REFERENCES Booking(bookingId)
);

CREATE TABLE Cancellation(
cancellationId 	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
bookingId 	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
cancellationDate 	date NOT NULL,
refundAmount 	number(7,2) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (cancellationId),
FOREIGN KEY (bookingId) REFERENCES Booking(bookingId)
);

CREATE TABLE CheckInLuggage(
luggageId  	varchar(5) NOT NULL,
checkLuggageId   number NOT NULL,
checkInTime  	varchar(10) NOT NULL,
weight 		number(5,2) NOT NULL,
color 		varchar(15) NOT NULL,
status  	varchar(15) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (luggageId)
);

CREATE TABLE Purchase(
purchaseDate  	date NOT NULL,
passengerIC  	varchar(14) NOT NULL,
itemId 		varchar(5) NOT NULL,
qty  		number NOT NULL,
amount 		number(7,2),
PRIMARY KEY (purchaseDate, passengerIC, itemId),
FOREIGN KEY (passengerIC) REFERENCES Passenger(passengerIC),
FOREIGN KEY (itemId) REFERENCES Item(itemId)
);

CREATE TABLE ItemOrder(
itemOrderId varchar(5) NOT NULL,
prebookDate date NOT NULL,
totalAmount number(7,2) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (itemOrderId)
);

CREATE TABLE PrebookDetail(
itemOrderId varchar(5) NOT NULL,
itemId varchar(5) NOT NULL,
qty number NOT NULL,
amount number(7,2),
PRIMARY KEY (itemOrderId, itemId),
FOREIGN KEY (itemOrderId) REFERENCES itemOrder(itemOrderId),
FOREIGN KEY (itemId) REFERENCES Item(itemId)
);

CREATE TABLE BookingDetails(
wayId 	number NOT NULL,
bookingId varchar(5) NOT NULL,
passengerIC varchar(14) NOT NULL,
itemOrderId varchar(5),
policyId varchar(5) NOT NULL,
flightId varchar(4) NOT NULL,
seatId varchar(8) NOT NULL,
checkLuggageId  number,
PRIMARY KEY (wayId, bookingId, passengerIC),
FOREIGN KEY (bookingId) REFERENCES Booking(bookingId),
FOREIGN KEY (passengerIC) REFERENCES Passenger(passengerIC),
FOREIGN KEY (policyId) REFERENCES InsurancePolicy(policyId),
FOREIGN KEY (flightId) REFERENCES Flight(flightId),
FOREIGN KEY (seatId) REFERENCES Seat(seatId),
FOREIGN KEY (itemOrderId) REFERENCES ItemOrder(itemOrderId)
);

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER trg_calc_purchase_itemPrice
BEFORE INSERT ON Purchase
FOR EACH ROW
DECLARE
    v_itemPrice Item.itemPrice%TYPE;
    v_totalAmount NUMBER(7,2);
BEGIN
    -- Get the item price from the Item table
    SELECT itemPrice INTO v_itemPrice
    FROM Item
    WHERE itemId = :NEW.itemId;

    -- Calculate the total amount for the inserted PrebookDetail
   v_totalAmount := v_itemPrice * :NEW.qty;
   :NEW.amount := v_totalAmount;
    
END;
/

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER trg_calc_prebook_itemPrice
BEFORE INSERT ON PrebookDetail
FOR EACH ROW
DECLARE
    v_itemPrice Item.itemPrice%TYPE;
    v_totalAmount NUMBER(7,2);
    v_recordExists NUMBER;
BEGIN
    -- Get the item price from the Item table
    SELECT itemPrice INTO v_itemPrice
    FROM Item
    WHERE itemId = :NEW.itemId;

    -- Calculate the total amount for the inserted PrebookDetail
   v_totalAmount := v_itemPrice * :NEW.qty;
   :NEW.amount := v_totalAmount;


    -- Check if the itemOrderId exists in the ItemOrder table
    SELECT COUNT(*) INTO v_recordExists
    FROM ItemOrder
    WHERE itemOrderId = :NEW.itemOrderId;
    
    IF v_recordExists > 0 THEN
        -- Record Exists
        UPDATE ItemOrder
        SET totalAmount = totalAmount + v_totalAmount
        WHERE itemOrderId = :NEW.itemOrderId;
    ELSE
        -- Record does not exist
        INSERT INTO ItemOrder values (:NEW.ItemOrderId, TO_DATE(SYSDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD'), v_totalAmount);
    END IF;
    
END;
/
